    A Concubine's Farewell Letter

    When Pèng served beside her lady's seat, hearing these words, tears fell like rain. She immediately rose and went inside. That night, when the lady was asleep, she secretly went out to meet her lover. They looked at each other and wept. She then said to him, "Just as we were enjoying ourselves, now there is a long separation! Is it heaven or man? Why has it come to this?" He replied, "I am forced by my mother and elder brother. I will only return temporarily. In three or four months, we will plan to meet again. You must calm your mind. Take care of your sleep and meals. Do not grieve uselessly, which only damages your beautiful appearance." Pèng, with tears in her eyes, said, "Be careful on your journey. Arrive home early. Come back when you have the chance. Do not leave me for long. My ugly body belongs to you. If you remember me, do not abandon me far away. Even on the day of my death, it would still be like a living year." She bowed twice to him and said, "This is the last time I see you. I cannot come out tomorrow." He also choked up and watched her leave.

    The next morning, Pèng sent Fu Fu to knock on the door, carrying a letter and giving him a pair of shoes made of black silk and a pair of silk stockings. The letter read:

    Pèng, a lowly concubine, respectfully writes to you, my dear brother: Pèng, a lowly concubine, cannot serve you for long. Now that I am heading east, I have nothing to give you. I made these rough shoes and silk stockings to show my slight intention. May your steps wherever they lead be as if I were still by your side. My endless thoughts cannot be fully expressed in writing. I bow my head and seal this letter, tears streaming down my face.

    After he had finished reading, he could only weep, and then he gathered and locked the documents in his book case.     In the Ruoya River, ten thousand red flowers bloom, but how can it compare to the auspiciousness of your family's twin lotus? Han and Guo have different demeanors when drunk and sober, while Ying and Huang each adorn themselves with light and dark makeup. In vain the painter's brush, wasted the poet's embroidered heart.     Tall and graceful, the green canopy provides shade, one kind of grace, two different kinds of beauty. The swallow after washing harmonizes with the beauty, the colorful phoenix slightly drunk leans on the literary flute. If they could speak, they would surely envy each other; even if they were without feeling, they would still be enchanting.     251

    At the summit of Mount Taihu, along the banks of the Ruoya Creek, the autumn waters ripple gracefully, their gentle waves caressing the beauty of the season. Beneath the shade of lush greenery, fair maidens stand close together, their perfumed shoulders touching. How can the deep cups withstand the frequent toasts? Their faces, radiant like the morning glow, vie in their beauty. Indeed, they are like the virtuous and pure beings, untouched by worldly affairs. They are praised for their graceful and charming demeanor, likened to the legendary couple Fengtai and Xiangshi, who ascended to heaven together. Even the finest paintings and silk cannot capture the clarity and elegance of their presence. The mandarin ducks, known for their fidelity, are said to envy them and prefer to be near them, symbolizing mutual affection and loyalty. Yet, their hearts are filled with sorrow, their emotions entangled and hidden, like threads buried in the mud.

    The young man, listening to their words, felt ashamed of his own inadequacy. He stepped forward and bowed, saying, "Your grace and charm are truly unparalleled; you are indeed the epitome of talent and beauty, a true match for the talented women of the past!" The maiden, named Ping, took her embroidered handkerchief and bowed in thanks, saying, "I dare not accept such praise! I dare not!" As the wine was drunk and the moon rose bright, the lady retired to her chambers, deeply asleep. Ping then approached the young man, recounting the events of the previous day's chess game, and sighed, "If it weren't for the peach blossom falling, the lady would have seen us! What shall we do? What shall we do?" The young man replied, "This is fate! But if it weren't for your quick thinking and adaptability, the cracks would have been exposed, and how could we have reunited? How perilous! How perilous!" Ping said, "The lady scolded me yesterday for passing through the garden, and I dare not go there again. What I regret most is our long separation, but now we are fortunate to meet again."

    252

    复被匪人百端间阻，当为兄屈己下之，冀回其意。兄且忍耐，勿自忧煎。然此亦由兄私之之过也！《论语》曰：‘惟女人与小人为难养也！近之则不逊，远之则怨。’不可不加之意也。”盖微讽生宠春鸿、兰苕事以箴之，生惭悚交并，莫知为对。娉自此深居简出，杳不相闻。生亦踧踖不安，若有芒刺在背，凡遇内集，多却不来。娉虽谬为敛迹，而益重幽思，故于鸿、苕，特加礼待，但其所欲，举以赠焉。尔后二人俱囿娉术中，夙怨冰释，翻为之用，第生未知耳。

    踽踽月余，无聊特甚。正忧闷中，忽福福送新莲数房来，且报鸿、苕释憾，早晚可以相见。生闻之，手舞脚蹈，不任欢情，因以蜀笺写所赋夏景闺情十首，为小引于前以答娉。其词曰：

    孤馆无聊，睡起块坐，不见贤淑，岂止鄙吝复生而己哉！谩成闺思十首奉寄，一则以见此情之拳拳，一则时自省览，犹佳丽之在侧也。

    Explanation

    252

    The young man was repeatedly obstructed by unscrupulous people, and he was advised to humble himself before his elder brother, hoping to change his mind. The elder brother was urged to endure and not to worry excessively. However, this situation was also due to the elder brother's excessive favoritism! As the Analects says: "Only women and small people are difficult to deal with! If you are close to them, they become insolent; if you keep your distance, they become resentful." This cannot be ignored. It was subtly criticizing the young man's favoritism towards Chunhong and Lantiao as a warning. The young man felt ashamed and terrified, not knowing how to respond. Peng thereafter lived a secluded life, rarely seen or heard from. The young man also felt uneasy and restless, as if there were thorns on his back. Whenever there were family gatherings, he often did not attend. Though Peng mistakenly retreated, he grew even more introspective. Thus, he treated Chunhong and Lantiao with special courtesy, giving them whatever they desired. Thereafter, the two were both ensnared by Peng's influence, their long-standing grudges melted away, and they turned against him, though the young man was unaware of this.

    For over a month, the young man was particularly bored. In his distress, he suddenly received a message from Fu, who brought several new lotus plants and reported that Chunhong and Lantiao had reconciled and could meet soon. Upon hearing this, the young man danced with joy, unable to contain his happiness. He then wrote ten poems about summer scenes and the emotions of a lady, and composed a preface to send to Peng. The preface read:

    Alone in a desolate inn, I sit idly after waking from sleep, missing the presence of a virtuous and graceful woman. How could it be merely a matter of petty greed and stinginess! I hastily composed these ten poems of a lady's thoughts to send to you. They serve to express the sincerity of my feelings and to remind myself to reflect upon them, as if a beautiful lady were by my side.

    253

    香闺晓起泪痕多，卷理青丝发一緺。十八云鬟梳掠遍，更将鸾镜照秋波。

    侍女新倾盥面汤，轻攘雪腕立牙床。都将隔宿残脂粉，洗在金盆彻底香。

    红绵拭镜照窗纱，画就双蛾八字斜。莲步轻移何处去？阶前笑折石榴花。

    深院无人刺绣慵，闲阶自理凤仙丛。银盆细捣青青叶，染得春葱指甲红。

    薰风无路入珠帘，三尺冰绡怕汗粘。低唤小鬟扃绣户，双弯自濯玉纤纤。

    爱唱红莲白藕词，玲珑七窍逗冰姿。只缘味好令人羡，花未开时已有丝。

    雪为容貌玉为神，不遣风尘涴此身。顾影自怜还自叹，新妆好好为何人？

    月满鸿沟信有期，暂抛残锦下鸣机。后园红藕花深处，密地偷来自浣衣。

    明月婵娟照画堂，深深再拜诉衷肠。怕人不敢高声语，尽在殷勤一炷香。

    阔幅罗裙六叶裁，好怀知为阿谁开？温生不带风流性，辜负当年玉镜台。

    Explanation

    253

    In the fragrant boudoir, tears stain the morning air; she combs her black hair into a single braid. Her cloud-like tresses are thoroughly arranged, and she gazes into the phoenix mirror at her autumnal eyes.

    The maid pours fresh water for her to wash her face, standing with her white wrists raised on the platform. She removes the leftover makeup from the previous night, and the water in the golden basin smells thoroughly fragrant.

    She wipes the mirror with red cotton and looks through the window, drawing her eyebrows in an eight-shaped slant. With graceful steps, she wonders where she is going, and smiles as she picks a pomegranate flower before the steps.

    In the secluded courtyard, she is lazy about embroidery, tending to clusters of begonias on idle steps. She finely pounds green leaves in a silver basin, dyeing her nails red like spring onions.

    The warm breeze cannot enter the pearl curtain, and she fears sweat will stick to her fine silk. She calls a young maid to close the embroidered door, washing her delicate and white hands.

    She enjoys singing songs about red lotus and white lotus, her seven orifices graced with icy beauty. Her beauty is envied, evident even before she is fully developed.

    Her appearance is snow-like, her spirit jade-like, and she does not allow worldly troubles to soil her body. She looks at her reflection, feeling sorry for herself and sighing, wondering for whom her new makeup is perfect.

    The full moon surely has a time to cross the great divide, and she temporarily puts aside leftover brocade and lowers the loom. In the back garden with deep red lotus flowers, she secretly steals them to wash her clothes.

    The bright, graceful moon illuminates the painted hall, and she deeply bows and pours out her heart. Afraid of people, she does not dare to speak loudly, expressing her feelings through a diligent stick of incense.

    Her wide silk skirt is cut into six pieces, and she wonders for whom her good mood is for. Wen does not have a flirtatious nature, betraying the jade mirror stand from the past.

    254

    诗后，复写一词，名《青玉案》：

    合欢花下曾相见，犹记把毫题彩扇；自别佳人冰雪面，朝思暮想，倚门挨户，无虑千来遍。 灵犀一点悬春线，残梦惊回梁上燕！惆怅佳期成又变！云笺都是蝇头字，难写张生怨！

    书毕，付福赍去。娉得之，启诵。而鸿、苕偶来，问曰：“小姐所咏诗，谁人之作？乃尔俊丽耶！”娉汪然流泪曰：“久有心事，思与渠辈谈之，屡欲吐辞，复嗫嚅而止。”鸿等同声应曰：“某辈贱流，受小姐厚爱多矣！但可为地，当尽力以报。”娉曰：“此魏生诗也。吾之遇彼，渠辈颇详。爰自尔日重阴之游，几于狼狈。若为夫人见之，我无措身之地，赖汝调护，遂得无他。今不见生者，一月矣，非惟我念之深，生亦思我尤切。彼此隔越，谁与为谋？”二人起谢曰：“今夫人受戒，日坐佛阁，诵内典，家政悉小姐所权，苟有欲为，畴敢喘息？若有异议，某等任之。脱不践言，鬼神临鉴！”娉曰：“若然，吾何恨。

    Explanation

    254

    After the poem, another piece of writing was composed, titled Qing Yu An:

    We once met under the happy flower, and I still remember holding the brush to write on a colorful fan; since parting from the beauty with her icy and snowy face, I have thought of you from morning till night, standing by the door and leaning against the house, countless times. A touch of spiritual connection like a spring thread, a broken dream awakens the swallows on the beam! Feeling sorrowful as the good time becomes and changes! The cloud-like letter is filled with tiny writing, hard to write the grievances of Zhang Sheng!

    After finishing, the writing was entrusted to Fu to deliver. Ping received it and began to read. Meanwhile, Hong and Tao happened to come and asked, "Whose work is the poem that the young lady has recited? It is so beautiful and elegant!" Ping burst into tears and said, "I have long had something on my mind, and I wanted to talk about it with you, but I hesitated to speak." Hong and the others replied in unison, "We are lowly and unworthy, but we have received much kindness from the young lady! If you need us, we will do our best to help." Ping said, "This poem was written by Wei. My encounter with him, you all know quite well. Since that day when we went out in the heavy rain, we were nearly in a difficult situation. If the mistress had seen us, I would have nowhere to hide, but thanks to your care, I was able to escape unharmed. Now that I have not seen Wei for a month, not only do I miss him deeply, but he also thinks of me even more intensely. Being separated from each other, who can we turn to for help?" The two stood up and thanked her, saying, "Now that the mistress has taken a vow, she sits in the Buddha hall every day, reciting Buddhist scriptures, and the management of the household is entirely in the young lady's hands. If there is anything we can do, we dare not hesitate. If there is any disagreement, we will take responsibility. If we fail to keep our word, may the spirits witness!" Ping said, "If that is the case, what do I have to regret?"

    255

    ”是夕，始复就生，相与如故矣。或偎红倚翠，尽云雨之欢；或举白弄琴，极从容之乐。不觉流光奄冉，七夕又临。娉请于夫人，于内堂结彩楼乞巧，瓜果罗列，肴羞备陈。夫人谓娉曰：“久不见汝作诗词，今夕天上佳期，人间良夜，或诗或词，随汝所为。吾当召魏生来，与汝讲论，庶有新益。”娉唯命。于时生至。夫人曰：“世谓今宵天孙赐巧，小女辈未能免俗，谩设瓜果之筵。亦尝命之赋小诗，以纪佳节，竟未知曾就否？”娉即前应曰：“适奉命，缀得七言绝句二首。”遂出诸袖间，墨痕犹湿。夫人接看毕，递与生曰：“小女拙诗，提举无吝见教。”生读竟曰：“宋若华姊妹之俦，诚不易得也！鹏虽不敏，当亦效颦，第恐白雪阳春，难为属和耳！”娉诗曰：

    255

    That night, they began to return to their former selves, and they were together as before. Some embraced each other closely, enjoying the pleasures of intimacy; others raised cups and played the qin, indulging in the utmost leisure and ease. Unaware of the fleeting passage of time, the Qixi Festival arrived again. The young woman, Pīng, requested permission from the lady to set up a colorful pavilion in the inner hall for the Qixi Festival, arranging fruits and delicacies. The lady said to Pīng, "I haven't seen you compose poetry or lyrics for a long time. Tonight is a special occasion in the heavens and a beautiful night on earth. Whether it's a poem or a lyric, do as you wish. I will summon Mr. Wèi to discuss your work with you, so that you might gain new insights." Pīng complied. At that time, Mr. Wèi arrived. The lady said, "It is said that tonight the Heavenly Grandson grants skill, and the young ladies could not avoid the custom. We have set up a fruit banquet. I also asked them to compose a short poem to commemorate the festival, but I don't know if they have done so yet?" Pīng immediately stepped forward and replied, "Just now, I was instructed and composed two seven-character quatrains." She then took them out from her sleeves, and the ink was still wet. The lady took them, read them, and passed them to Mr. Wèi, saying, "Here is my daughter's humble poetry. Please do not hesitate to offer criticism or advice." Mr. Wèi finished reading and said, "She is truly a match for the sisters Song Ruohua and Song Ruoxue!     256

    梧桐枝上月明多，瓜果楼前艳绮罗。不向人间赐人巧，却从天上渡天河。

    斜亸香云倚翠屏，纱衣先觉露华零。谁云天上无离合？看取牵牛织女星。

    鹏和诗曰：

    流云不动鹊飞多，微步香尘满袜罗。若道神仙无配耦，怎教织女渡银河？

    娟娟新月照围屏，井上梧桐一叶零。今夕不知何夕也，双星错道是三星。

    讵意好事多乖，会难离易。次早，生收家问，报母讣音，竟不及荣上提举之任，而丁忧之行逼矣。夫人乃召边妪告之曰：“吾有一切己事相托，未审能为我周全乎？”妪避席曰：“愿闻何事？苟可用情，当为极力。”夫人曰：“娉娉年长，欲觅一快婿。斧柯之任，相属如何？”妪笑曰：“老拙久怀此意，但未敢形言。今夫人门下，自有其人，而欲他谋，徒费齿颊，真所谓道在迩而求诸远也。”夫人曰“得非谓魏生乎？佳则佳矣，然有说焉：生少年高擢，扬历仕途，若以归之，势必携去。

    Explanation

    256

    The moon shines brightly on the paulownia branches, and before the pavilion of melons and fruits, silks gleam in radiant hues. It does not grant skill to mortals, but instead sends beings across the Milky Way from heaven.

    Slanting fragrant clouds lean against the emerald screen, and the silk robe first senses the falling dew. Who says there is no parting or reunion in heaven? Look at the stars of the Cowherd and the Weaver Girl.

    Peng replies with a poem:

    The flowing clouds remain still, yet many magpies fly. With delicate steps, fragrant dust fills the silk socks. If the immortals have no partners, how could the Weaver Girl cross the Milky Way?

    The slender new moon shines on the surrounding screen, and a single leaf of the paulownia falls by the well. Tonight, I do not know what night it is, for the two stars are mistaken for three.

    Who would have thought that good things are often thwarted, and meetings are hard while partings are easy? The next morning, the son returned home to receive the news of his mother’s death, and thus was unable to take up the post of Rongshang, for the mourning journey was now pressing upon him. His wife then summoned the matchmaker and said, “I have a personal matter to entrust to you—may I ask if you can assist me thoroughly?” The matchmaker bowed and said, “I would be glad to hear what it is. If it is within my power, I shall do my utmost.” The wife said, “Pengping has grown older, and I wish to find her a capable and suitable husband. Are you willing to take on this task of matchmaking?” The matchmaker smiled and said, “I have long harbored this very thought, but I dared not speak of it. Now, within your household, there is already a suitable person. To seek elsewhere would be a waste of words—truly, this is what is meant by 'the path is near, yet one seeks it far away.'" The wife said, “Are you not referring to Wei-sheng? He is indeed fine, but I must say—this young man has risen high in official ranks, and if he were to marry her, he would surely take her with him.”

    257

    吾止有此一息，时刻不面，尚且念之，若嫁他乡，宁死不忍！正为向者生来时，乃母惠书及此，且举昔日指腹之言。我欲答书，深思而止。是以对生亦绝口不曾道及者，非背盟也。今萧夫人弃养，生又得官，他日当自有佳人，求为匹配，丑女不足以奉箕帚也。吾不欲面谈，烦妪委曲达及，使之他图。我若不明言，彼又胶于前语，如之何其不两误耶！”妪如教喻生。生曰：“余久知之，彼则迟疑未判，今言若此，明说不谐。况寒门重罹荼毒，行色匆匆，陨越之余，宁暇为计？虽然，此先堂意也，烦妪善为我辞夫人。岂不闻圣人有言：‘自古皆有死，民无信不立。

    Explanation

    257

    I have only this life, and even without seeing each other, I still think of you. If I were to marry someone in a different place, I would rather die than submit! This is because since my birth, my mother's kind letter reached me, and it mentioned the previous promise made by pointing to the bellies of pregnant women. I wanted to reply, but after deep thought, I stopped. Therefore, I have not spoken to him about it, but this is not a breach of the alliance. Now that Lady Xiao has passed away, and he has obtained an official position, one day there will be a good match for him, seeking to be paired. I am not worthy to serve as a wife. I do not want to discuss this face-to-face. Please instruct the old woman to convey this message indirectly, so that he may consider other options. If I do not speak clearly, he will be stuck on the previous words. How can this not lead to mutual error? The old woman followed the instructions and conveyed the message to him. He said, "I have known this for a long time, but he has been hesitant and undecided. Now that you say this, clearly stating it will not work. Besides, a humble family suffering greatly, with hurried preparations, after such a disaster, how could we have time to plan? Although, this is the intention of my late father. Please instruct the old woman to convey this message to Lady Xiao. Do you not hear what the sage said: 'Since ancient times, everyone has to die, but without trust, a people cannot stand.'"

    258

    ’既奉初言，息壤在彼，天地鬼神，昭布森列。岂可以吾母既亡，背盟弃好？且闾阎下贱，尚不食言，曾谓小君，而可失信？妪若以义责之，庶或可允。万一秦晋能谐，当奉千金为寿。”妪曰：“我哀王孙而缓颊，岂望报哉？”遂去，备以言反复劝于夫人。夫人曰：“妪虽巧为说客如苏、张，其如吾不听何！”妪见如此，不敢复言。退而告生。生忍泪曰：“死生契阔，从此始矣！” 乃促装，亟为归计。娉闻之，与春鸿、秋蝉辈，伺夫人困睡，潜于柏泛堂设宴，召生入，为别。生至相持，魂飞魄丧，呜咽不自胜。

    Explanation

    258

    Having already made my initial statement, the land of peace lies there, and the heavens and earth, gods and spirits, are clearly displayed and arranged. How can I break an alliance and discard friendship after my mother's passing? Even the common people, who are considered lowly, do not break their word; how much more so, then, for a wife, and can she be untrustworthy? If the old woman holds me accountable based on righteousness, perhaps she will be satisfied. If there is a chance that Qin and Jin can reconcile, I will offer a thousand gold pieces as a gift." The old woman said, "I am merely pleading for the sake of the young master, not expecting any reward!" She then left, preparing to repeatedly advise the lady with these words. The lady said, "Even if the old woman is a skilled orator like Su Qin or Zhang Yi, what can be done if I do not listen?" Seeing this, the old woman dared not speak further. She then informed the young man. The young man held back his tears and said, "Parting ways in life and death, this marks the beginning!" He then hastily prepared and made immediate plans to return. The betrothed heard this and, along with Spring Swallow and Autumn Cicada, waited for the lady to fall asleep, secretly setting up a banquet in the Bofan Hall and summoning the young man to bid farewell. When the young man arrived, they embraced, his soul and spirit lost, sobbing uncontrollably.

    259

    鸿等亦哽塞，不能仰视。娉乃举杯于生前，拜曰：“兄行，不来矣！平昔与兄，一日不握手，此恨何堪。矧今守制三年，仳离千里，不谐伉俪，从此途人。惟兄节哀顺变，保摄金玉之躯。服阕上官，别议佳偶，宗祧为重，勿久鳏居。妾命薄春冰，身轻秋叶，云泥异路，浊水清尘。然既委身于君子，岂再托体于他人。以死为期，言犹在耳，行当毕命穷泉，寄骸空木。长恨悠悠，曷其有极！平时兄屡命我歌，每每忸怩而止，今死生永诀，岂可复辞？我试讴之，兄其侧耳。政唐人所谓‘一声《河满子》，双泪落君前’ 也。”乃歌《踏莎行》一阕云：

    Explanation

    259

    The group of people also choked up, unable to look up. The maiden then raised a cup in front of the gentleman and bowed, saying: "My brother, you will not come back! In the past, whenever we were apart for even one day, I could not shake hands, and this pain was unbearable. Especially now, observing the mourning for three years, separated by a thousand miles, unable to be together as husband and wife, from now on we are strangers. Please grieve moderately and adapt to the changes, taking care of your precious health. After the end of the mourning period, consider another good match, for the continuation of the family line is important, and do not remain a widower for too long. My life is as thin as spring ice, my body as light as autumn leaves, like heaven and earth apart, like muddy water and clear dust. However, since I have entrusted my body to a gentleman, how could I entrust it to others? I have set death as the deadline, the words are still ringing in my ears, I will end my life in the depths of the earth, leaving my body in an empty coffin. Enduring sorrow, how long will it last? In the past, my brother often asked me to sing, but I was bashful and stopped. Now, with this final farewell, how can I refuse? I will sing one song, please listen. It is like the Tang poem that says, 'A single sound of He Manzi, tears fall before you.'"

    260

    随水落花，离弦飞箭，今生无处能相见！长江纵使向西流，也应不尽千年怨！盟誓无凭，情缘无便，愿魂化作衔泥燕。一年一度一归来，孤雌独入郎庭院。

    歌讫，大恸数声，蓦然仆地，左右扶掖，良久乃苏，竟夕不成欢而罢。来早，娉乃破所照匣中鸾镜，断所弹琴上冰弦，并前时手帕，遣福福持去付生，为相思纪念。福福艴然曰：“小姐赋禀温柔，幽娴贞静，其性不可及，一也。天姿美艳，绝世无双，其貌不可及，二也。歌词流丽，翰墨清新，其才调不可及，三也。谙晓音律，善措言辞，其聪明不可及，四也。至于考究经史，评论古今，纚纚然如贯珠，洒洒然若霏雪。下至女事，更不在言。

    Explanation

    260

    Falling flowers follow the stream, arrows fly from the bowstring, in this life there is no place where we can meet again! Even if the Yangtze River were to flow westward, the thousand-year-old grudges would still not be resolved! Vows made without substance, and the lack of favorable circumstances for our love, I wish my soul could transform into a swallow that carries mud. Once a year, the lone female swallow returns to my lover's courtyard.

    After singing, she burst into tears and fell to the ground. Those around her helped her up, and after a long while, she regained consciousness. That night, she could not find joy and ended the gathering. The next morning, Ping broke the mirror in her box, snapped the strings of her zither, and sent her handkerchief to her lover, Fu Fu, as a memento of her longing. Fu Fu angrily said: "Miss is gentle and virtuous, refined and chaste, her nature is unmatched, first. Her beauty is extraordinary, unmatched in the world, her appearance is unmatched, second. Her lyrics are graceful, her writings are fresh, her talent is unmatched, third. She understands music, speaks eloquently, her intelligence is unmatched, fourth. As for her knowledge of history and literature, her comments on ancient and modern times, they are like pearls strung together, like snowflakes falling gently. Even down to women's affairs, she is even more skilled, but that is not worth mentioning."

    261

    矧又为蓟公之孙，平章之女，母有邢国之贤，弟有令尹之贵，四德俱备，一族同推。行配高门，岂无佳婿？顾乃逾墙钻穴，轻弃此身，恋恋魏生，甘心委质，流而为崔莺莺、王娇娜淫奔之女，以辱祖宗。且生累然衰绖，五内崩摧，以此与之，毋乃不可！诚所谓既不能以礼自处，又不能以礼处人。妾实耻之，无面目将去也。”娉吁气长叹曰：“尔自事吾，小心谨慎，我亦怜汝，不啻已生。来往十年，未尝暂舍，然尚不知我心，犹有此论，则纷纷外议，无怪其然。与其负谤而生，莫若捐躯而死。”乃取白练，将自缢，福遽止之，急足递去。

    Explanation

    261

    Considering further, as the granddaughter of Jil Gong and the daughter of Pingzhang, with a mother as virtuous as the ruler of Xing state and a brother as noble as a high-ranking official, all four virtues are present, and the entire family holds her in high esteem. Should she not have a good match for such a noble lineage? Yet, she secretly meets and lightly abandons herself, deeply attached to Wei Sheng, willingly submitting to him, flowing into the ranks of the infamous lovers Cui Yingying and Wang Jiaona, bringing shame to her ancestors. Moreover, the husband is in a state of mourning, his heart broken, and marrying under such circumstances is surely inappropriate! Indeed, this is what it means to fail both in maintaining propriety oneself and in upholding it in others. The woman truly feels ashamed and has no face to leave. Pings sighed and said, "You have served me with care and diligence, and I also love you as if you were my own. We have been together for ten years, without ever parting. Yet, you still do not understand my feelings and still hold such views. Then, the many external criticisms are no wonder. Rather than live with dishonor, it would be better to die." She then took a piece of white cloth, intending to hang herself. Fu quickly stopped her and sent someone to go away urgently.

    262

    生收置行李中，入辞夫人。夫人赠白金五十两，生固却不受。夫人曰：“知不成礼，聊见微情。想读礼之余，剩有闲暇，毋惜惠音，以慰老朽。”生跪曰：“数年门下，深荷恩慈，岂特待我如宾，真乃视余犹子，死生肉骨，镂胆铭肝。方获微官，冀图少报，不幸祸延先妣，遗弃诸孤，守制东还，远违懿范，素心曷已，黄发是期！”俯首阶庭，不胜沾洒。夫人亦感怆，使鸿呼娉出别，促之至再，坚不肯来。生亦不苦请，盖不忍与之见也。遂行。

    其年秋，麟果中浙江乡试，夫人喜动颜色，曰：“双莲之祥验矣。”遂改重阴亭为瑞莲亭。明年，赴春官，亦得捷，授陕西之咸宁尹，乃挈家偕行。娉自离生后，柳悴花憔，香消玉减，终日不食，达旦不眠，咄咄书空，盈盈滴泪。兼之道途顿撼，陆路艰难，抵县浃旬，息将垂绝。夫人忧损特甚，莫晓其致病之由。研问家人，鸿等始略言其概。夫人懊恨违盟，势已无及，但百端宽喻，使之勉进汤药而已。

    Explanation

    262

    The man packed his belongings and entered to bid farewell to his wife. The wife presented him with fifty taels of silver, but he firmly refused to accept it. The wife said, “I know this is not a proper gift, but I offer it as a small token of affection. I hope that, in your spare time after studying the rites, you will not hesitate to write to me, to comfort this old woman.” The man knelt and said, “For many years under your care, I have deeply felt your kindness and mercy. You have not merely treated me as a guest, but have regarded me as your own child. You have given me life, and I have engraved your kindness in my heart and carved it into my very soul. Only now, having obtained this minor official position, do I hope to repay you in some small way. Unfortunately, misfortune has befallen my late mother, leaving me to abandon my children and return eastward to observe mourning rites, far from your noble example. My sincere heart has not yet found rest, and I shall wait until my hair turns white.” He bowed his head on the steps, overwhelmed with emotion. The wife was also moved to grief and sent Hong to summon Ping to say goodbye, urging her twice, but she firmly refused to come. The man also did not press her, for he could not bear to see her. Thus, he departed.

    That autumn, Lin indeed passed the Zhejiang provincial examination. His wife was overjoyed and said, “The omen of the double lotus has come true.” She then renamed the pavilion from Chongyin Pavilion to Rui Lian Pavilion, the Auspicious Lotus Pavilion. The following year, he took the imperial examination and also succeeded, being appointed as the magistrate of Xianning in Shaanxi. He then took his family with him and set out. Since parting from Lin, Ping had grown pale and frail, her beauty faded, her fragrance lost, her jade-like form diminished. She ate nothing all day and did not sleep through the night, writing in the air in frustration, her tears flowing endlessly. Moreover, the journey was jarring, and the land route was difficult. Upon reaching the county after ten days, her breath was nearly gone. The wife was greatly distressed, unable to understand the cause of her illness. She inquired thoroughly from the family, and Hong and the others finally gave a vague account of the situation. The wife regretted breaking their promise, but it was now too late. She could only try every possible way to comfort and persuade her, urging her to take her medicine.

    263

    又月许，将属纩之先一日，沐浴梳饰，具衣帨如常时，于母前拜曰：“儿不幸！疾疢弥留，死在朝夕，母恩未报，饮恨黄泉。赖有灵昭，可为终养，愿夫人割不可忍之恩，勿以女子自苦也。”又语麟曰：“吾弟聪明才智，早掇巍科，步武青云，前程远大，家门有幸，父母有光。但愿早寻佳耦，以养夫人。姊命薄年促，不及见贤弟耸壑昂霄，徒以死相累耳！我殁后，千万勿焚，谋一抔之土以权殡。俟贤弟解官，北归幽州，携骨还葬，则志愿永毕。”返室，抚福福曰：“我将溘先朝露，只在朝夕。汝善事夫人，勿以我为念。”又有手书嘱春鸿曰：“为我以是寄谢魏生，俾知我为泉下客矣。

    Explanation

    263

    After about a month, on the day before I was to be wrapped in the silk cloth to test my breath, I bathed and groomed myself, prepared my clothing and wiping cloth as I would on any ordinary day, and bowed before my mother, saying: "Alas, my misfortune! My illness has lingered, and death is imminent. I have not yet repaid my mother's kindness, and I shall die with sorrow in the underworld. Thanks to your kindness and clarity, I may be cared for until the end. I beg Madam to restrain this unbearable sorrow and not burden yourself as a woman." I then spoke to Lin, saying: "My younger brother is intelligent and talented, having early attained high honors in the imperial exams, ascending to lofty positions, with a promising future. Our family is fortunate, and our parents are honored. I only wish he would find a good match soon to support Madam. My fate is weak and my years are short; I did not live to see my virtuous younger brother rise to great heights, and I am only a burden with my death! After I die, please do not burn me, but arrange for a small plot of earth for a temporary burial. Wait until my virtuous younger brother resigns from office and returns north to Youzhou, then carry my bones back for burial, and my wishes will be forever fulfilled." Returning to my room, I comforted Fu Fu, saying: "I shall die before the morning dew, only a matter of days away. You must treat Madam well, and do not think of me." I also wrote a letter to Chunhong, saying: "On my behalf, convey this thanks to Weisheng, so that he may know I am now a guest of the nether world."

    264

    ”鸿谨藏而慰之曰：“小姐平生颖悟，通达过人，虽在女流，深知道理。亦尝贱焦仲卿伉俪之伤生，鄙荀奉倩夫妻之灭性，岂今日忘之，而自蹈其覆辙乎？且生一去，遽绝音徽，虽在制中，谅亦谋配。今红叶频来，纷纭旁午，天下多奇男子、美丈夫，以小姐才貌配之，孰所不愿？何必魏生，然后快意？况夫人垂暮，爱女只小姐一人，万一果致沦亡，尊怀何以堪处？窃为小姐不取也！惟小姐不以人废言，曲听鄙语，翻然省悟，以理自遣，则非春鸿之幸，亦非小姐之幸，实夫人之大幸也。

    Explanation

    264

    Hong carefully concealed himself and comforted her, saying: "Miss, your lifelong sharpness of mind and surpassing wisdom are well known. Though you are a woman, you deeply understand the principles of morality and reason. You have also looked down upon the tragic deaths of Jiao Zhongqing and his wife, and scorned the self-annihilation of Xun Fengqian and his wife. How could you now forget these things and yourself tread the same path of ruin? Moreover, since he has gone, he has abruptly cut off all communication. Though you are in mourning, surely you would be seeking a suitable match. Now red leaves are coming frequently, in a confused and overlapping manner—there are many extraordinary men and handsome husbands in the world. Who would not wish to be matched with you, given your talent and beauty? Why must it be Wei Sheng in order to be satisfied? Furthermore, your mother is now old, and her only beloved daughter is you. If she were to be lost, how could your esteemed heart bear it? I secretly think this course of action is not acceptable to you! If only you would not dismiss my words because of me, but would listen kindly to my humble words and suddenly come to a realization, and console yourself with reason—then it would not be the happiness of Spring Hong, nor the happiness of the young lady, but truly the great happiness of the lady [your mother]."

    265

    ”娉曰：“嘻！尔过矣！吾岂世间痴淫女子，不知命者之流乎？吾之与生，盖不偶也。彼此在母，先已缔盟。厥后二家，果生男女，斯言斯誓，不爽毫厘，则天意人事，断可知矣。岂料萱亲钟爱，不果命以归生，虽出恩慈，不免负约。且女子事人，惟一而已，苟图他顾，则人尽夫也，鬼神其谓我何？《诗》曰：‘谷则异室，死则同穴。’吾之心事，生实知之。春鸿虽厚我念我，然君子爱人以德，不可以姑息也。”言讫，泪落如雨。鸿亦惨惨而出。至晚竟逝。麟以漆棺殓之，殡于开元寺僧舍，期任满载归瘗焉。

    无何，县有剧盗，遁于襄阳，官遣胥吏康铧者往彼捕之，春鸿乃出娉缄白麟，俾因铧寄去与魏生。麟拆览之，乃集唐人诗成七言绝句十首，与生为诀之词也。麟以白母。夫人曰：“人已逝矣，勿违其意。”遂命寄去。其诗曰：

    Explanation

    265

    Peng said, "Ah! You are mistaken! Am I not a woman of intelligence and understanding of my fate, rather than a foolish and ignorant one? I and Sheng are not fated to be together. Our parents had made a pact before we were born. Later, when the two families had children, the words and vows they made were fulfilled without deviation. Thus, it is clear that this was the will of heaven and the course of human affairs. Who could have predicted that my mother favored someone else and did not fulfill her promise to marry me to Sheng? Even though she acted out of kindness, it still felt like a breach of the agreement. Moreover, a woman should have only one partner. If one seeks multiple partners, then everyone becomes a husband, and what would the spirits think of such behavior? The Book of Songs says, 'We may live in different rooms, but in death we will share the same grave.' My feelings and intentions, Sheng truly knows. Although Chunhong cares deeply for me, true love should be based on virtue and not indulgence." After saying this, she cried profusely. Chunhong also left in a despondent manner. That night, she passed away. Lin prepared her body for burial with a lacquered coffin, and she was temporarily placed in a temple at Kaiyuan Temple. After the official period, her body was returned home for burial.

    Shortly after, there was a notorious bandit in the county who fled to Xiangyang. The authorities sent an official named Kang Hua to capture him. Chunhong then sent a letter to Lin, asking him to send it to Wei Sheng via Kang Hua. Lin read the letter and found it contained ten seven-character quatrain poems composed from Tang dynasty poets, which were farewell messages to Wei Sheng. Lin then ordered the letter to be sent. His mother said, "She is already gone. Do not go against her wishes." The poems read:

    266

    两行清泪语前流，千里佳期一夕休！倚柱寻思倍惆怅，寂寥灯下不胜愁！

    相见时难别亦难，寒潮惟带夕阳还。钿蝉金雁皆零落，离别烟波伤玉颜。

    倚阑无语倍伤情，乡思撩人拨不平。寂寞闲庭春又晚，杏花零落过清明。

    自从消瘦减容光，云雨巫山枉断肠！独宿孤房泪如雨，秋宵只为一人长。

    纱窗日落渐黄昏，春梦无心只似云。万里关山音信断，将身何处更逢君？

    一身憔悴对花眠，零落残魂倍黯然！人面不知何处去，悠悠生死别经年。

    真成薄命久寻思，宛转峨眉能几时？汉水楚云千万里，留君不住益凄其。

    魂归冥溟魄归泉，却恨青娥误少年。三尺孤坟何处是？每逢寒食一潸然。

    物换星移几度秋，鸟啼花落水空流！人间何事堪惆怅？贵贱同归土一丘。

    Explanation

    266

    Two rows of tears flow before speaking, a thousand-mile rendezvous ends in one night! Leaning on a pillar, pondering increases sorrow, lonely under the lamp, unable to bear the sorrow!

    Meeting is hard, parting is even harder, cold waves only bring the setting sun back. The gold cicadas and golden geese have all fallen, farewell amidst the misty waves, wounding the fair face.

    Leaning on the railing, speechless, the sorrow is doubled, homesickness stirs the heart, unable to be settled. Lonely in the quiet courtyard, spring has come late, the apricot blossoms fall, passing Qingming.

    Since then, I have become thinner, my beauty diminished, the clouds and rain of Mount Wu, in vain, breaking the heart! Sleeping alone in an empty room, tears flow like rain, the autumn night seems to stretch endlessly, for the sake of one person.

    The woven window, as the sun sets, gradually turns to dusk, spring dreams, without intent, are like clouds. Across ten thousand miles of mountains and rivers, messages are cut off, where will I meet you again?

    Wasted and weary, sleeping among the flowers, the scattered soul is even more sorrowful! The face of the person is unknown, where has it gone? Separated by life and death, for many years.

    Truly, a life of misfortune, long pondered, the graceful eyebrows will last for how long? The Han River and Chu clouds, ten thousand miles apart, unable to keep you, the sorrow increases.

    The soul returns to the depths of darkness, the spirit returns to the springs, regretting the young girl who has misled the youth. Where is the three-foot grave? Every time the Cold Food Festival comes, tears flow.

    Objects change, stars shift, how many autumns have passed? Birds cry, flowers fall, water flows in vain! What in the world is worth being sorrowful about? Rich and poor, all return to the same mound of earth.

    267

    一封书寄数行啼，莫动哀吟易惨凄。古往今来只如此，几多红粉委黄泥。

    生家居苫块，度日如年，追念旧欢，遽成陈迹，然犹不知娉之死也。因赋《摸鱼儿》一阕忆之。词曰：

    记当年、浪游江海，湖山佳处频到。绯桃红杏春光媚，骏马骄嘶驰道。亲曾造，拜第一仙人，听鼓《朝飞操》，风流音耗。纵水隔蓬壶，浪翻银汉，青鸟解相报。 徒自悼，忆刹那人情好，万千心事难告！天涯回首成陈迹，还想绿依红靠。空洒泪，叹暑往寒来，绿鬓愁成皓！何时偎抱？把月下鸾箫，花间凤管，细写断肠套。

    词成，盖略述与娉相遇颠末。方拟谋人寄去，忽康铧自陕来，得娉凶问，并所集古句绝诗，读之哀怨，闷而复苏。乃于岘山堕泪碑傍，为位以哭，酹酒以祭，且出娉前时所赠破镜、断弦，仰天誓曰：“子既为我捐生，我又何忍相负？惟当终身不娶，少慰芳魂。”祭文就录于左云：

    Explanation

    267

    A letter containing a few lines of tears, do not let sorrowful songs easily become sad. Throughout history, it has always been like this; how many beautiful women have become dust.

    Living in a thatched hut, each day feels like a year, recalling past joys, they quickly become memories. Yet still unaware of Ping's death, therefore, composing a poem titled "Mò Yú Ér" to remember her. The poem says:

    Remembering those days, wandering the rivers and seas, frequently visiting beautiful lakes and mountains. Peach blossoms and red apricots in spring are charming, and swift horses neigh proudly on the road. I once visited, bowed to the first immortal, and listened to the drumming of "Cháo Fēi Cāo," the news of people's kindness, and countless heart affairs are hard to tell! Looking back from the ends of the earth, everything becomes a memory, still hoping to rely on green and red. Only shedding tears, lamenting the passing of summer and the coming of winter, green hair turning white with worry! When will we embrace again? Playing the moonlit lüè箫 and the flower-blooming fèng管, carefully writing the heart-wrenching suite.

    The poem completed, it roughly describes the meeting with Ping. Just planning to send it, suddenly Kang Hua came from Shaanxi, bringing news of Ping's death and her collected ancient verses. Reading it, feeling sorrowful, I became depressed and then revived. Then at the Xian Mountain Weeping Stone, I set up an altar to cry and pour wine to offer, also taking out the broken mirror and broken strings that Ping had given me before. Swearing to the sky: "Since you have sacrificed yourself for me, how can I bear to betray you? I will remain unmarried for life, slightly comforting your soul." The memorial text is recorded as follows:

    268

    维大元至正十二年月日，钜鹿魏鹏，颛以清酌肴羞之奠，遥祭于故贾氏云华小娘子之灵。呜呼！天地既判，即分阴阳。夫妇攸合，人道之常。从一而殒，是谓贞良，二三其德，是曰淫荒。昔我参政，暨先平章，僚友之好，金兰其芳。施及寿母，与余先堂，义若姊妹，闺门颉颃。适同有妊，天启阙祥，指腹为誓，好音琅琅。乃生君我，二父继亡。君留浙水，我返荆襄。彼此阔别，各居一方。日月流迈，逾十五霜，千里跋涉，访君钱塘。佩服慈训，初言是将，冀遂曩约，得谐姬姜。因缘浅薄，遂堕荒唐，一斥不复，竟成参商。呜呼！君为我死，我为君伤！天高地厚，莫诉衷肠！玉容花貌，宛在目傍。断弦裂镜，零落无光。人非物是，徒有涕滂！悄悄寒夜，隆隆朝阳，佳人何在？令德难忘！曷以招子？谁为巫阳？曷以慰子？鳏居空房。庶几斯语，闻于泉乡。岘山郁郁，汉水汤汤，山倾水竭，此恨未央。呜呼小姐，来举余觞。尚飨！

    Explanation

    268

    In the twelfth year of the Zhizheng era of the Great Yuan, on this day, Wei Peng from Julu humbly offers clear wine and delicacies as a sacrifice, offering this from afar to the spirit of the late Lady Yunhua of the Jia family. Alas! When heaven and earth were divided, yin and yang were separated. The union of husband and wife is a constant of human nature. To remain loyal until death is called virtue and goodness; to be fickle in one's virtue is called debauchery. My former colleague, the late Chancellor, and I, as well as our mutual respect for our mothers and fathers, were as close as sisters, standing together in the inner chambers. Coincidentally pregnant at the same time, a sign of auspiciousness from heaven, we made a promise by pointing to the bellies, with clear and loud words. And thus we were born, with both fathers passing away. You stayed in Zhejiang, I returned to Jingxiang. We parted ways, each living in a different place. Months and years passed, more than fifteen winters. Traveled thousands of miles to visit you in Qiantang. Followed your kind teachings, initially planning to do so, hoping to fulfill our old promise, to marry as husband and wife. Due to thin karmic connections, we fell into absurdity. Once criticized, never to be reconciled, becoming like the stars Shen and Shang. Alas! You died for me, I mourn for you! Heaven is high, earth is thick, no one can express my inner feelings! Your beautiful face and delicate features are still vivid in my eyes. The broken string and shattered mirror, now scattered and without light. People change, things remain, only tears flow! Quiet cold nights, rising suns. Where is the beautiful lady? Her noble virtues are unforgettable! How can I summon you? Who will be the medium for me? How can I comfort you? Living alone in an empty room. Perhaps these words will reach you in the netherworld. Mount Xian is lush, the Han River flows abundantly. Even if mountains collapse and rivers dry up, this sorrow will never end. Alas, Lady, come and raise my cup. May you enjoy the sacrifice!

    269

    未久，生服满赴都，升除陕西儒学正提举，阶奉议大夫。而麟尹咸宁，瓜期尚未及代，复得相见，升堂拜母，而夫人益老矣。见生，只加悲悔。旧仆若脱欢辈，亦有物故者，惟春鸿诸姬，一一无恙。生询知殡宫所在，即往痛哭，以手叩墓门曰：“云华，魏寓言在此。想子平生精灵未散，岂不能为《华山畿》乎》”生是夕，宿公署，似梦非梦，仿佛见娉来曰：“天果从人愿乎？”生忘其死也，遽拥抱之。娉曰：“兄勿见持，当有奉告。”生方悟其鬼也，因问之曰：“子已谢世，今安得来耶？”娉曰：“妾死后，冥司以我无过，命入金华宫，掌笺奏之任。今冥君感子不娶之言，以为义高刘庭式。且曰：‘不可使先参政盛德无后。’将命我还魂，而屋舍已坏。今议假他尸，尚未有便。数在冬末，方可遂怀，彼时复得相聚也。”语毕，倏然飞去。生惊觉，但见淡月侵帘，冷风拂面，四顾凄然，泣数行下。遂成《疏帘淡月》词一阕以吊娉。词云：

    Explanation

    269

    Not long after, the protagonist completed his mourning period and went to the capital, where he was appointed as the Supervisor of Confucian Education in Shaanxi and granted the rank of Fengyi Dafu. Meanwhile, his mother, Lin, was still serving as the magistrate of Xianning, and her term had not yet ended. They were reunited, and he ascended the hall to pay respects to his mother, who had grown even older. Upon seeing him, she only added sorrow and regret. Among the old servants, such as Tuohuan, some had passed away, but Chunhong and the other concubines were all unharmed. The protagonist inquired about the location of the funeral house and went there to mourn, knocking on the tomb gate with his hand and saying, "Yunhua, Wei Yuyan is here. I believe your spirit has not yet dispersed; could you not compose a Huashanjiji for me?" That night, he stayed at the government office, and in a dream-like state, he saw Ping approach and ask, "Has heaven indeed granted our wishes?" He forgot that she was dead and embraced her. Ping said, "Brother, do not hold me; I have something to tell you." The protagonist realized she was a ghost and asked, "You have already passed away; how can you be here now?" Ping replied, "After my death, the underworld found me blameless and assigned me to the Jinhua Palace, where I am responsible for drafting documents. Now, the ruler of the underworld is moved by your words about not marrying, deeming your righteousness as high as Liu Tingshi's. He also said, 'We cannot allow the former chancellor's virtue to have no descendants.' He intends to return me to life, but the house has been destroyed. We are now discussing borrowing another's body, but it is not yet convenient. The time is in late winter, when we may finally be reunited." After her words, she suddenly flew away. The protagonist awoke with a start, seeing faint moonlight seeping through the curtains and a cold wind brushing against his face. Looking around, he felt desolate, and tears streamed down. He then composed a poem titled "Sparse Curtain and Faint Moon" to mourn Ping. The poem reads:

    270

    西湖皓月，从前岁别来，凡回圆缺？何处凄然，怕近暮秋时节！花颜一去成终古，洒西风，泪流如血！美人何在？忍看残镜！忍看残玦！ 忽今夕，分明梦里，陡然相见，手携肩接。微启朱唇，耳畔低声儿说：冥君许我返魂也，教同心罗带重结。醒来惊怪，还疑又信，枕寒灯灭。

    生到任，不觉雪花飘粉，梅蕊舒琼，兔走乌飞，又当腊月。有长安丞宋子璧者，一室女，年及笄，忽暴卒；已三日，复苏，不认其父母，曰：“我贾平章女云华，今咸宁县尹贾麟姊也。死已二年，数当还魂。今假汝女之尸，其实非汝女也。”父母讶其声音不类，言语不伦，正疑怪间，女即径入贾尹宅，如素曾到者。见夫人及尹，道还魂甚详。夫人与麟察之：声音语笑，娉也；举止态度，娉也。然尚未信。

    Explanation

    270

    The moon over West Lake, how many times has it waxed and waned since our last parting? Where is the place of sorrow, fearing the approach of late autumn? Once the beautiful face is gone, it is forever lost; the west wind weeps, and tears flow like blood! Where is the beautiful woman? How can one endure looking at the broken mirror! How can one endure looking at the broken jade! Suddenly tonight, clearly in a dream, I meet her unexpectedly, holding hands and leaning on each other. She gently opens her red lips and whispers softly in my ear: "The ruler of the underworld has allowed me to return to life, teaching us to rebind the heartstrings with a double knot." I awaken in surprise and wonder, still doubting but also believing, the pillow is cold and the lamp is extinguished.

    Upon arriving at my post, I notice snowflakes drifting like powder, plum blossoms blooming with jade-like petals, the hare and the crow flying swiftly, and it is already the month of the twelfth. There is a daughter of the magistrate of Chang'an named Song Zibi, who had reached the age of marriage, suddenly died; after three days, she revived, not recognizing her parents, saying, "I am the daughter of Chancellor Jia, Yunhua, and the elder sister of the county magistrate of Xianning, Jia Lin. I have been dead for two years, and it is my turn to return to life. Now I am using your daughter's body, but in truth, I am not your daughter." Her parents were astonished by her voice, which did not resemble theirs, and her words, which seemed out of place. As they were still in doubt, the girl immediately entered the magistrate Jia's residence as if she had been there before. She met the magistrate's wife and the magistrate, recounting her return to life in great detail. The magistrate's wife and Jia Lin examined her: her voice and laughter, her movements and demeanor, were all like those of the deceased. Yet they still did not fully believe.

    271

    须臾，入其寝室，呼春鸿诸婢妾名字，索其存日遗物，丝发皆不谬，始深信之。盖咸宁与长安，俱西安在城属县，廨宇相邻。宋丞亦闻贾尹到任时，其姊氏亡故，然还魂之事，世所罕有，乃与其妻陈氏同诣贾宅取回。女子坚不肯出，且诟骂曰：“何为妄认他人家女为女耶？”宋夫妇无计，遂叹息而返。夫人曰：“此天作之合也。”乃报魏生。生亦以梦中见娉事告贾母子。夫人忻忭难言，于是命媒妁，通殷勤，再缔前盟，重行吉礼。生执雁帛往亲迎焉。夫人暨春鸿、兰苕等俱往送。娉花烛之夕，真处子也。枕上与生话旧，一事不遗。

    Explanation

    271

    In a short while, he entered her bedroom, calling out the names of Chunhong and her maidservants, searching for her belongings from the past. Not a single thread or hair was wrong, and only then did he deeply believe it. Xianning and Chang'an are both counties within the city of Xi'an, and their government buildings are adjacent. Cheng Song also heard that when Director Jia took office, his sister had passed away. The matter of resurrection is rare in the world, so he and his wife Chen went to Director Jia's house to retrieve her. The girl firmly refused to come out, and she scolded and cursed, saying, "Why would you falsely recognize a girl from another family as your own?" Cheng and his wife had no solution, so they sighed and returned. The lady said, "This is a match made by heaven." So he reported to Wei Sheng. Wei Sheng also told Director Jia and his son about the dream in which he saw the betrothal. The lady was extremely happy and could hardly express her joy, so she ordered the matchmakers to convey her goodwill, re-establish the previous engagement, and perform the wedding ceremony again. Wei Sheng held the ceremonial gifts and went to fetch her. The lady and Chunhong, Lan Tiao, and others all went to see her off. On the night of the wedding, she was truly a virgin. She talked about old times with Wei Sheng in bed, not missing a single detail.

    272

    翌日，设宴于提举公廨后堂。宋丞一门，亦与礼席，因询丞：“女何名？”乃知呼为月娥。又得之老门子云：“廨宇后堂，旧有扁名洒雪，盖取李太白诗 ‘清风洒兰雪’之义，为前任提举取去，今无矣。”遂悟伍相庙梦中神云者，上句言成婚之地，下句言其妻之名。生遍以告座人，知神言之验，喧传关中，莫不叹异。有赋《永遇乐》词以庆生者，因录于此：

    Explanation

    272

    The following day, a banquet was held in the rear hall of the superintendent's office. The Song family, including the official, were also given a place of honor. The scholar asked the official, "What is your daughter's name?" and learned that she was called Yue'e. He also heard from an old gatekeeper that the rear hall used to have a signboard named "Suxue," which took its meaning from a line by Li Bai's poem "Clear wind sprinkles orchid snow," and was taken away by the former superintendent. Thus, the scholar realized that the deity in the Wu Zixu Temple had foretold the location of his marriage and the name of his wife. He told everyone present, and knowing that the words of the deity were true, the news spread throughout Guanzhong, and everyone marveled at the unusual event. There was a poem titled "Eternal Joy" composed to celebrate the occasion, which is recorded here:

    273

    倾国名姝，出尘才子，真个佳丽。鱼水因缘，鸾凤契合，事如人意。贝阙烟花，龙宫风月，谩托传书柳毅。想传奇、又添一段，勾栏里做《还魂记》。 稀稀罕罕，奇奇怪怪，凑得完完备备。梦叶神言，婚谐腹偶，两姓非容易。牙床儿上，绣衾儿里，浑似牡丹双蒂。问这番、怎如前度，一般滋味？

    生后与娥产三子，皆列显官。生仕至大禧宗禋院使、兵部尚书，年八十三方死。娥亦封鄯国夫人，寿七十九而殁，与生合葬焉。生与娥平昔吟咏赓和之作，多至千余篇，题曰《唱随集》；酸斋贯云石为序于其前，生夫妇自序于其后，载于别录，此不著云。

    (完）

    Explanation

    273

    A beauty who can topple a nation, a talented man who transcends the mundane, truly a pair of exquisite beauties. Their bond is as natural as fish and water, and their union is as harmonious as a phoenix and a crane. Everything goes as they wish. In their luxurious and enchanting environment, they entrust the legendary Liu Yi to deliver their messages. It seems that this story adds another chapter to the legend, performed in a traditional Chinese theater as "The Story of the Return from the Dead." Rare and precious, strange and unusual, everything comes together perfectly. The dream fulfills divine words, and their marriage is a predestined union, not easily achieved. In their intimate setting, they are like the twin buds of a peony. Ask how this time compares to the last, and the experience is the same.

    After their union, the couple had three sons, all of whom became prominent officials. The man rose to the position of Grand Director of the Imperial Ancestral Temple and Minister of War, dying at the age of eighty-three. The woman was also ennobled as Lady of Shan and lived to seventy-nine before passing away, and she was buried alongside her husband. The man and woman had many poems and verses they composed together, totaling over a thousand pieces, titled "The Collection of Singing and Following." The preface was written by Guan Yunshi of Suanzai, and the couple wrote their own preface at the end, which is recorded in other works, but is not mentioned here.
